## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population size (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various density-dependent and density-independent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth where rate is proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreases logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth with minimum viable population threshold (strong Allee effect)'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth model'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Saturating per-capita growth rate with contest competition'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Generalized density-dependent growth with fractal or allometric scaling'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with time-varying environmental conditions'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with time-varying capacity', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with changing carrying capacity over time'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Polynomial expansion of density-dependent effects including higher-order interactions'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or rational form 1/(1 + c*P) reducing growth at high density
- Allee effect / cooperative dynamics → quadratic or cubic terms in P creating multiple equilibria (e.g., P*(P-c1)*(c2-P))
- Logarithmic saturation in growth → log(K/P) term indicating Gompertz-type diminishing returns
- Allometric scaling of metabolic processes → fractional power laws P**c with c between 0 and 1 (e.g., 2/3 or 3/4)
- Separability test: if dP_dt depends only on P (not t), the system is autonomous and time-invariant
- Sign change in dP_dt at specific P values → polynomial roots indicating equilibrium points and stability structure
- Per-capita growth rate (dP_dt / P) decreasing linearly with P → classic logistic signature
- Delayed or lagged environmental effects → explicit time dependence multiplied by population terms

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.13870625668024555*(-1 + P/8.038138014396704)*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*P/(1 + exp(-8.038138014396704*(-0.5894251550796137 + P)))
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote α = 0.13870625668024555, a = 8.038138014396704, b = 70.01799944958296, d = 0.5894251550796137.

**Term 1:** α*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 2:** α*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 3:** α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(-d + P)))

Let me combine Terms 1 and 2:
α*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] = α*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a)
= (α/a) * P² * (1 - P/b)
= (α/a) * (P² - P³/b)

So the GT simplifies to:
**(α/a) * P² * (1 - P/b) + α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d)))**

Computing α/a = 0.13870625668024555/8.038138014396704 ≈ 0.01725...

So GT = **A*P² + B*P³ + α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))** where A = α/a, B = -α/(a*b).

This is a **cubic polynomial in P** plus a **sigmoid-like term** (specifically P times a logistic sigmoid).

Note that α*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d))) = α*P * σ(a*(P-d)) where σ is the logistic function.

Also note: log(c*exp(x) + 1) is the softplus function, and its derivative is the sigmoid. But the GT has P*sigmoid, not softplus.

However, we can write: if we have c*log(e^{aP} * c' + 1), this is a softplus, not P*sigmoid. These are NOT the same.

So the GT has the form: **quadratic in P (P² and P³ terms) + P·sigmoid(P)**.

This is a very specific functional form. Let me check candidates for matching basis functions.

The key question: can any candidate produce P² + P³ + P/(1+exp(-a(P-d)))?

The sigmoid term P/(1+exp(...)) is NOT the same as log(exp(...)+1) (softplus). They are fundamentally different functions.

Let me also check: can sin/cos terms match the sigmoid? No - sin is periodic, sigmoid is not. These are linearly independent.

Can exp terms match? exp(cP) is monotonically increasing/decreasing, while P·sigmoid saturates to linear. Not equivalent.

Can log(P²c+1) match? This is a logarithmic function, not equivalent to P·sigmoid.

So I need candidates that explicitly contain P/(1+exp(...)) or an equivalent form.

None of the candidates contain an explicit sigmoid term P/(1+exp(...)). 

The closest are candidates with log(c*exp(P*c) + 1) which is softplus, NOT sigmoid times P.

Let me verify: is there any algebraic relationship? The derivative of softplus is sigmoid, but softplus itself is not P*sigmoid.

For large P: softplus ≈ aP + const, while P*sigmoid ≈ P. For small P: softplus ≈ log(2), while P*sigmoid ≈ 0. These are fundamentally different.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT** because none contain the P/(1+exp(...)) sigmoid term, and no combination of the available basis functions (polynomials, sin, cos, exp, log, softplus) can exactly reproduce P·sigmoid(P).

Let me do a quick scan to confirm no candidate has 1/(1+exp(...)):

Scanning all 69 candidates... None contain 1/(1+exp(...)) or P/(1+exp(...)). The closest are log(c*exp(Pc)+1) terms (softplus), which are NOT equivalent.
